[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of the Issue[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe evaluation report identifies a heap-buffer-overflow at line [0m[1;36m327[0m[39m in [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/shadowsocks/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m` during JSON parsing. The vulnerability is a classic [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moff-by-one error in bounds checking when processing UTF-[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m surrogate pairs.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue stems from incorrect bounds checking for the [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpre-increment-and-dereference operator `*[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. When this operator is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mused:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The pointer is incremented FIRST[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Then the incremented location is dereferenced[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFor N such operations, we need at least N+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m bytes available from the current [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mposition [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcurrent byte + N forward bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. However, the vulnerable code checks for [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monly N bytes.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerable Code Pattern[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAt line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m, the code checks `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m` before performing [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m `*[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstate.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` operations:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m: Two increments [0m[1;39m([0m[39mchecking for [0m[32m'\\' and '[0m[39mu'[0m[1;39m)[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m324[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m327[0m[39m: Four more increments [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreading hex digits[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhen exactly [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m bytes remain, the check passes, but the 6th operation at line [0m[1;36m327[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreads [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte past the buffer boundary, causing the reported overflow.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Comprehensive Fix Strategy[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m - Surrogate Pair Handling[0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** `[0m[35m/src/shadowsocks/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m323[0m[39m`[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change Required:**[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Current [0m[1;39m([0m[39mVULNERABLE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'\\' || [0m[32m([0m[32m*++ state.ptr[0m[32m)[0m[32m != '[0m[39mu' ||[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Fixed:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'\\' || [0m[32m([0m[32m*++ state.ptr[0m[32m)[0m[32m != '[0m[39mu' ||[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification:** This directly addresses the vulnerability reported at line [0m[1;36m327[0m[39m. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe surrogate pair handling performs [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m pre-increment-and-dereference operations, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequiring at least [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes to be available. This follows the same pattern as the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch already applied at line [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mchanged from `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` to `< [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m` for [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m operations[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Additional Fixes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPreventive - Same Vulnerability Pattern[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhile the evaluation report focuses on line [0m[1;36m327[0m[39m, the codebase contains identical [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability patterns at other locations. These should also be fixed to prevent [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msimilar issues:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m:** `[0m[35m/src/shadowsocks/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m306[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mAlready patched in [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgood_patch.diff[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Current: `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fixed: `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Context: Basic unicode escape sequence `\uXXXX` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m operations[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m:** `[0m[35m/src/shadowsocks/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m602[0m[39m`[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Current:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Implementation Steps from Initial Codebase[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Apply the primary fix at line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m:**[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change the bounds check from `< [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m` to `< [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m`[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This directly resolves the reported vulnerability at line [0m[1;36m327[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Reapply the fix from good_patch.diff at line [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m:**[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change from `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` to `< [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m`[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This fix was in the previous patch but must be reapplied to the initial [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Apply preventive fixes at lines [0m[1;36m602[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m618[0m[39m, and [0m[1;36m633[0m[39m:**[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Increment each threshold value by [0m[1;36m1[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - These follow the same vulnerable pattern and should be fixed proactively[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal and Surgical:** Only modifies integer constants in bounds checks, no [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic changes[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Consistent Pattern:** Applies the same N+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m rule across all similar code [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocations[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Complete Coverage:** Addresses all instances of the vulnerable pattern, not [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjust the reported one[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Maintains Functionality:** Preserves all parsing capabilities including:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Unicode escape sequences[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - UTF-[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m surrogate pair handling[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - JSON literal values [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue, false, null[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Two-pass parsing structure[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Error reporting[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No changes to parsing algorithms:** Only boundary checks are adjusted[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No changes to data structures:** All variables, types, and memory layouts [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremain identical[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No changes to control flow:** Same branching and iteration logic[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No changes to string processing:** Same escape sequence handling and unicode [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msupport[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Compatible with fuzzing:** The harness code remains unchanged and continues to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest the same code paths[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Evaluation Report[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Direct fix for line [0m[1;36m327[0m[39m:** The primary vulnerability is eliminated by [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrecting the bounds check at line [0m[1;36m323[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Prevents [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte overflow:** With `< [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m` check, we ensure all [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m read operations [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstay within bounds[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Matches the patch pattern:** Follows the same approach as good_patch.diff [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mincrement threshold by [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Comprehensive coverage:** Also fixes similar vulnerabilities that could be [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggered by other fuzzer inputs[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect:** Slightly more conservative boundary checking [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrejects input [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mearlier than before[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation:** This is actually desired behavior. The original code had off-by-one[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merrors that allowed invalid access. The new checks correctly enforce buffer [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundaries according to the actual read operations performed.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Impact on Valid Input:** [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m. Valid JSON inputs will still parse correctly. The [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfix only rejects malformed or truncated inputs that would have caused buffer [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflows.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Impact on Error Messages:** Error reporting remains unchanged. The same error [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmessages are displayed when boundary checks fail.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase already demonstrates correct boundary checking in several locations:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m462[0m[39m: `state.ptr < [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before accessing `state.ptr[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m478[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m481[0m[39m: Check after incrementing, before dereferencing[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m656[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m664[0m[39m: Safe increment-check-use pattern[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix aligns the vulnerable locations with these existing correct patterns.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
